This is done because policy rules are purely additive and policy determinations\n\t// can be made on the basis of those rules that are found.\n\tRulesFor(ctx context.Context, user user.Info, namespace string) ([]rbacv1.PolicyRule, error)\n\n\t// VisitRulesFor invokes visitor() with each rule that applies to a given user in a given namespace, and each error encountered resolving those rules.\n\t// If visitor() returns false, visiting is short-circuited.\n\tVisitRulesFor(ctx context.Context, user user.Info, namespace string, visitor func(source fmt.Stringer, rule *rbacv1.PolicyRule, err error) bool)\n}\n\n// ConfirmNoEscalation determines if the roles for a given user in a given namespace encompass the provided role.\nfunc ConfirmNoEscalation(ctx context.Context, ruleResolver AuthorizationRuleResolver, rules []rbacv1.PolicyRule) error {\n\truleResolutionErrors := []error{}\n\n\tuser, ok := genericapirequest.UserFrom(ctx)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"no user on context\")\n\t}\n\tnamespace, _ := genericapirequest.NamespaceFrom(ctx)\n\n\townerRules, err := ruleResolver.RulesFor(ctx, user, namespace)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// As per AuthorizationRuleResolver contract, this may return a non fatal error with an incomplete list of policies. Log the error and continue.\n\t\tklog.V(1).Infof(\"non-fatal error getting local rules for %v: %v\", user, err)\n\t\truleResolutionErrors = append(ruleResolutionErrors, err)\n\t}\n\n\townerRightsCover, missingRights := validation.Covers(ownerRules, rules)\n\tif !ownerRightsCover {\n\t\tcompactMissingRights := missingRights\n\t\tif compact, err := CompactRules(missingRights); err == nil {\n\t\t\tcompactMissingRights = compact\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmissingDescriptions := sets.NewString()\n\t\tfor _, missing := range compactMissingRights {\n\t\t\tmissingDescriptions.Insert(rbacv1helpers.CompactString(missing))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmsg := fmt.Sprintf(\"user %q (groups=%q) is attempting to grant RBAC permissions not currently held:\\n%s\", user.GetName(), user.GetGroups(), strings.Join(missingDescriptions.List(), \"\\n\"))\n\t\tif len(ruleResolutionErrors) > 0 {\n\t\t\tmsg = msg + fmt.Sprintf(\"; resolution errors: %v\", ruleResolutionErrors)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn errors.New(msg)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\ntype DefaultRuleResolver struct {\n\troleGetter               RoleGetter\n\troleBindingLister        RoleBindingLister\n\tclusterRoleGetter        ClusterRoleGetter\n\tclusterRoleBindingLister ClusterRoleBindingLister\n}\n\nfunc NewDefaultRuleResolver(roleGetter RoleGetter, roleBindingLister RoleBindingLister, clusterRoleGetter ClusterRoleGetter, clusterRoleBindingLister ClusterRoleBindingLister) *DefaultRuleResolver {\n\treturn &DefaultRuleResolver{roleGetter, roleBindingLister, clusterRoleGetter, clusterRoleBindingLister}\n}\n\ntype RoleGetter interface {\n\tGetRole(ctx context.Context, namespace, name string) (*rbacv1.Role, error)\n}\n\ntype RoleBindingLister interface {\n\tListRoleBindings(ctx context.Context, namespace string) ([]*rbacv1.RoleBinding, error)\n}\n\ntype ClusterRoleGetter interface {\n\tGetClusterRole(ctx context.Context, name string) (*rbacv1.ClusterRole, error)\n}\n\ntype ClusterRoleBindingLister interface {\n\tListClusterRoleBindings(ctx context.Context) ([]*rbacv1.ClusterRoleBinding, error)\n}\n\nfunc (r *DefaultRuleResolver) RulesFor(ctx context.Context, user user.Info, namespace string) ([]rbacv1.PolicyRule, error) {\n\tvisitor := &ruleAccumulator{}\n\tr.VisitRulesFor(ctx, user, namespace, visitor.visit)\n\treturn visitor.rules, utilerrors.NewAggregate(visitor.errors)\n}\n\ntype ruleAccumulator struct {\n\trules  []rbacv1.PolicyRule\n\terrors []error\n}\n\nfunc (r *ruleAccumulator) visit(source fmt.Stringer, rule *rbacv1.PolicyRule, err error) bool {\n\tif rule != nil {\n\t\tr.rules = append(r.rules, *rule)\n\t}\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tr.errors = append(r.errors, err)\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc describeSubject(s *rbacv1.Subject, bindingNamespace string) string {\n\tswitch s.Kind {\n\tcase rbacv1.ServiceAccountKind:\n\t\tif len(s.Namespace) > 0 {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %q\", s.Kind, s.Name+\"/\"+s.Namespace)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %q\", s.Kind, s.Name+\"/\"+bindingNamespace)\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %q\", s.Kind, s.Name)\n\t}\n}\n\ntype clusterRoleBindingDescriber struct {\n\tbinding *rbacv1.ClusterRoleBinding\n\tsubject *rbacv1.Subject\n}\n\nfunc (d *clusterRoleBindingDescriber) String() string {\n\treturn %s\",\n\t\td.binding.Name+\"/\"+d.binding.Namespace,\n\t\td.binding.RoleRef.Kind,\n\t\td.binding.RoleRef.Name,\n\t\tdescribeSubject(d.subject, d.binding.Namespace),\n\t)\n}\n\nfunc (r := r.clusterRoleBindingLister.ListClusterRoleBindings(ctx); err != nil {\n\t\tif !visitor(nil, nil, err) {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tsourceDescriber := &clusterRoleBindingDescriber{}\n\t\tfor _, clusterRoleBinding := range clusterRoleBindings {\n\t\t\tsubjectIndex, applies := appliesTo(user, clusterRoleBinding.Subjects, \"\")\n\t\t\tif !applies {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trules, err := r.GetRoleReferenceRules(ctx, clusterRoleBinding.RoleRef, \"\")\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tif !visitor(nil, nil, err) subject,\n// and if true, the index of the first subject that applies\nfunc appliesTo(user user.Info, bindingSubjects []rbacv1.Subject, namespace string) (int, bool) {\n\tfor i, bindingSubject := range bindingSubjects {\n\t\tif appliesToUser(user, bindingSubject, namespace) {\n\t\t\treturn i, true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn 0, false\n}\n\nfunc has(set []string, ele string) bool {\n\tfor _, s := range set {\n\t\tif s == ele {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc appliesToUser(user user.Info, subject rbacv1.Subject, namespace string) bool {\n\tswitch subject.Kind {\n\tcase rbacv1.UserKind:\n\t\treturn user.GetName() == subject.Name\n\n\tcase rbacv1.GroupKind:\n\t\treturn has(user.GetGroups(), subject.Name)\n\n\tcase rbacv1.ServiceAccountKind:\n\t\t// default the It uses a RequestToRuleMapper interface to obtain policy rules for a user, then checks each rule using RuleAllows() to determine if the request matches any allowed policy rule.\\n\\n**Rule Resolution:**\\nThe DefaultRuleResolver (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go) is the primary implementation of the RequestToRuleMapper interface. It resolves PolicyRules for a given user by:\\n1. Collecting all applicable ClusterRoleBindings via ListClusterRoleBindings()\\n2. Collecting all applicable RoleBindings in the target namespace via ListRoleBindings()\\n3. For each binding whose subjects match the user, resolving the referenced Role or ClusterRole via GetRoleReferenceRules()\\n4. Accumulating all matching rules and returning them through RulesFor() and VisitRulesFor() methods\\n\\n**Subject Evaluation:**\\nThe SubjectAccessEvaluator (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/subject_locator.go) implements the SubjectLocator interface to provide the reverse lookup - determining which subjects can perform a given action. expose the authorization engine:\\n- SubjectAccessReview (subjectaccessreview/rest.go): Evaluates if a specific subject can perform an action\\n- LocalSubjectAccessReview (localsubjectaccessreview/rest.go): Namespace-scoped version of SubjectAccessReview\\n- SelfSubjectAccessReview (selfsubjectaccessreview/rest.go): Allows users to check their own permissions\\n- SelfSubjectRulesReview (selfsubjectrulesreview/rest.go): Returns all rules applicable to the current user\\n- Authorization storage (rest/storage_authorization.go): Coordinates the REST endpoints with the authorizer\\n\\n**Bootstrap Policies:**\\nThe bootstrappolicy package (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/) defines initial RBAC policies that are created during cluster system controllers with the \\\"system:controller:\\\" prefix\\n- namespace_policy.go: Defines Roles that are bootstrapped into reserved kube-* namespaces\\n\\n**Escalation Prevention:**\\nThe policy-based storage implementations enforce privilege escalation prevention:\\n- escalation_check.go: Provides utility functions (EscalationAllowed, RoleEscalationAuthorized, BindingAuthorized) to check authorization before allowing escalation\\n- role/policybased/storage.go: Wraps Role storage to prevent users from creating/updating Roles with permissions they don't possess\\n- clusterrole/policybased/storage.go: Wraps ClusterRole storage with similar escalation prevention, using fullAuthority (permissions to do anything) as the upper bound\\n- rolebinding/policybased/storage.go: Prevents users from binding Roles they cannot escalate (either by explicit escalate permission or by already having all the role's permissions)\\n-
